#<BL2 From Their Cold, Dead Hands>

    # BL2 From Their Cold, Dead Hands v1.0.0-prerelease
    # Licensed under Public Domain / CC0 1.0 Universal
    #
    # Enemies will always drop the specific gun/shield that they were using, on death, and
    # the gear quality for enemies has been much improved.  You will be fighting many
    # enemies which have blue and higher gear (including legendaries).  Badasses should
    # have better-quality gear than regular enemies, in general.  Creatures like Stalkers
    # and Skeletons, and devices like turrets, will NOT drop a shield, even if they spawn
    # with one.  Shielded loaders will drop shields, though.
    #
    # This mod requires that the UCP option "Skinpool Fixes (Don't uncheck this)" is
    # enabled!  If you want to run this without UCP, make sure to at least copy that
    # category over.

    #<Disable World Weapon/Shield Drops>

        # This section disables world drops for weapons and shields, so those items will
        # only drop from what the enemies are carrying.  Rather than deleting/disabling
        # the items entirely, we're changing them to draw from an ammo/money pool so that
        # the rest of the probabilities in the pools aren't affected.
        #
        # Note that this doesn't *completely* get rid of world weapon/shield drops, but it
        # should get rid of the vast majority of them.

        #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisableBalanced0"</key><value>",GD_Itempools.GeneralItemPools.Pool_Gear,BalancedItems[0].ItmPoolDefinition,,ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.LootablePools.Pool_Locker_Items_CashAndAmmo'"</value><on>

        #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisableBalanced1"</key><value>",GD_Itempools.GeneralItemPools.Pool_Gear,BalancedItems[0].InvBalanceDefinition,,None"</value><on>

            #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocEnemyDrop722"</key><value>",GD_Nast_Native_Soldier.Anims.Anim_Soldier_Warcry:BehaviorProviderDefinition_0.Behavior_AIChangeInventory_2,NewItemPoolList[0].ItemPool,,ItemPoolDefinition'GD_CustomItemPools_MainGame.Siren.VladofEpic'"</value><on>

            #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocEnemyDrop723"</key><value>",GD_Native_Soldier.Anims.Anim_Soldier_Warcry:BehaviorProviderDefinition_0.Behavior_AIChangeInventory_212,NewItemPoolList[0].ItemPool,,ItemPoolDefinition'GD_CustomItemPools_MainGame.Siren.VladofEpic'"</value><on>

        #</Badass Enemies>

    #</Enemy Pool Assignments>

    #<Bosses Use+Drop Their Unique Weapons>

        #<Guaranteed Boss Drops (non-weapon-using bosses)>

            set GD_Itempools.DropWeights.DropODDS_BossUniques:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1 

            set GD_Itempools.DropWeights.DropODDS_BossUniqueRares:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1 

            set GD_Itempools.DropWeights.DropODDS_BossUniquesRareSpawnMonster:ConstantAttributeValueResolver_0 ConstantValue 1 

        #</Guaranteed Boss Drops (non-weapon-using bosses)>

        #<Bosses Equip Uniques>

            #<Midge-Mong>

                # Midge is a generic Badass Midget, but he's also the only one to spawn in Southern
                # Shelf Bay, so we can just edit its equip pool.

                set GD_Itempools.Runnables.Pool_WarMong bAutoReadyItems True 

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocMidge0"</key><value>"Cove_P,GD_Population_Midget.Balance.PawnBalance_MidgetBadass,DefaultItemPoolList[0].ItemPool,,ItemPoolDefinition'GD_Itempools.Runnables.Pool_WarMong'"</value><on>

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocMidge1"</key><value>"Cove_P,GD_Population_PrimalBeast.Balance.Unique.PawnBalance_PrimalBeast_Warmong,DefaultItemPoolList,,()"</value><on>

            #</Midge-Mong>

            #<Captain Flynt>

                # Flynt ordinarily has a guaranteed Tinderbox drop, and a possible Thunderball Fists
                # drop.  We're combining those two, and Flynt will have one or the other (and drop
                # it).

                set GD_Itempools.Runnables.Pool_CaptFlynt bAutoReadyItems True 

                set GD_Itempools.Runnables.Pool_CaptFlynt BalancedItems ((ItmPoolDefinition=None,InvBalanceDefinition=WeaponBalanceDefinition'GD_Weap_Pistol.A_Weapons_Legendary.Pistol_Maliwan_5_ThunderballFists',Probability=(BaseValueConstant=1.000000,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000),bDropOnDeath=True),(ItmPoolDefinition=None,InvBalanceDefinition=WeaponBalanceDefinition'GD_Weap_Pistol.A_Weapons_Unique.Pistol_Bandit_3_Tenderbox',Probability=(BaseValueConstant=1.000000,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000),bDropOnDeath=True))

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisable0"</key><value>"SouthernShelf_P,GD_Population_Nomad.Balance.Unique.PawnBalance_Flynt,DefaultItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability,,(BaseValueConstant=0,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1)"</value><on>

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisable1"</key><value>"SouthernShelf_P,GD_Population_Nomad.Balance.Unique.PawnBalance_Flynt,DefaultItemPoolList[3].PoolProbability,,(BaseValueConstant=0,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1)"</value><on>

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisable2"</key><value>"SouthernShelf_P,GD_Population_Nomad.Balance.Unique.PawnBalance_Flynt,DefaultItemPoolList[2].PoolProbability,,(BaseValueConstant=1,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1)"</value><on>

            #</Captain Flynt>

            #<Bad Maw>

                # In vanilla BL2, Bad Maw doesn't have a specific weapon, but UCP adds
                # Deliverance.  So, we're going to go ahead and force him to equip that.

                set GD_Itempools.Runnables.Pool_Tumba bAutoReadyItems True 

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisable3"</key><value>"Frost_P,GD_Population_Nomad.Balance.PawnBalance_BadMaw,PlayThroughs[0].CustomItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability,,(BaseValueConstant=0,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1)"</value><on>

                #<hotfix><key>"SparkLevelPatchEntry-ApocDisable4"</key><value>"Frost_P,GD_Population_Nomad.Balance.PawnBalance_BadMaw,PlayThroughs[1].CustomItemPoolList[0].PoolProbability,,(BaseValueConstant=0,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1)"</value><on>

            #</Bad Maw>

        #</Bosses Equip Uniques>

    #</Bosses Use+Drop Their Unique Weapons>
